## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Kubernetes apimachinery runtime.Object Import Chain

## Your Task

Trace how k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/runtime.Object is imported and used across kubernetes/kubernetes. Find all Go source files in the core/v1 API types that implement runtime.Object by embedding TypeMeta and ObjectMeta, and the files in the API machinery that register these types into the scheme.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the crossrepo tracing domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/kubernetes--v1.32.0, sg-evals/client-go--v0.32.0, sg-evals/api--v0.32.0, sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd.

Create a file at `/workspace/answer.json` with your findings in the following structure:

```json
{
  "files": [

  ],

}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

Here is the complete, precise trace of how `k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/runtime.Object` is defined, implemented, and wired into the scheme for core/v1 types across `kubernetes/kubernetes`.

---

## 1. Interface Definition

**File:** `staging/src/k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/runtime/interfaces.go`, lines 336–339

```go
type Object interface {
    GetObjectKind() schema.ObjectKind
    DeepCopyObject() Object
}
```

Every API type registered with a `runtime.Scheme` must satisfy this two-method interface. The comment above it is explicit: *"Object interface must be supported by all API types registered with Scheme."*

---

## 2. Supporting Types in `apimachinery`

**File:** `staging/src/k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/runtime/types.go`, lines 38–43


**File:** `staging/src/k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/apis/meta/v1/types.go`, lines 42–57

```go
type TypeMeta struct {
    Kind       string `json:"kind,omitempty" ...`
    APIVersion string `json:"apiVersion,omitempty" ...`
}
```

This is what all external (versioned) API types embed. It carries the same `GetObjectKind()` semantics.

called from `addKnownTypes` in the core/v1 register |\n| `pkg/apis/core/install/install.go` | `Install(scheme)` calls `core.AddToScheme` + `v1.AddToScheme` + `SetVersionPriority`; `init()` applies this to `legacyscheme.Scheme` |\n| `pkg/api/legacyscheme/scheme.go` | Declares the global singleton `Scheme = runtime.NewScheme()` that all `install.go` init functions populate |\n\n---\n\n### The Complete Chain\n\n```\nruntime.Object (interfaces.go:336)\n  \u2193 GetObjectKind() satisfied by embedding:\nmetav1.TypeMeta (meta/v1/types.go:42)\n  \u2193 DeepCopyObject() satisfied by generated code in:\nzz_generated.deepcopy.go (both external and internal)\n  \u2193 types defined in:\nstaging/src/k8s.io/api/core/v1/types.go       (external)\npkg/apis/core/types.go                          (internal)\n  \u2193 registered by:\nstaging/src/k8s.io/api/core/v1/register.go    \u2192 scheme.AddKnownTypes({\"\",\"v1\"}, ...)\npkg/apis/core/register.go                      \u2192 scheme.AddKnownTypes({\"\",\"__internal\"}, ...)\n  \u2193 conversion/defaulting added by:\npkg/apis/core/v1/register.go\n  \u2193 all installed into global scheme by:\npkg/apis/core/install/install.go \u2192 init() \u2192 Install(legacyscheme.Scheme)\n  \u2193 global scheme lives at:\npkg/api/legacyscheme/scheme.go \u2192 Scheme = runtime.NewScheme()\n```"
